        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Last week we welcomed our new Graduates and Apprentices into Vodafone Group UK ‚ù§Ô∏è  Their first day was spent at Newbury HQ learning all about life at Vodafone and hearing from guest speakers, including some of our brilliant current grads and apprentices.

"It was an absolute joy and priviledge to welcome our new Group Graduates and Apprentices at their induction. As a Group HR Graduate myself, it was an amazing opportunity to be able to organise and bring our new Early careers cohort into the world of Vodafone, helping them settle and feel a real sense of belonging, which is exactly how I have felt in my first year of being here."

        attributed-text-segment-list__content-truncated" dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Subsea cables carry the vast majority of the world‚Äôs data traffic.
